        <div class="article-content js-article-content" role="main" itemscope itemprop="mainContentOfPage"> 
         <ul id="markdown-toc"> 
          <li><a href="#relationships-between-epics-and-issues" id="markdown-toc-relationships-between-epics-and-issues">Relationships between epics and issues</a> </li>
          <li><a href="#roadmap-in-epics" id="markdown-toc-roadmap-in-epics">Roadmap in epics <span class="badge-trigger ultimate"></span></a> </li>
          <li><a href="#permissions" id="markdown-toc-permissions">Permissions</a> </li>
          <li><a href="#related-topics" id="markdown-toc-related-topics">Related topics</a> </li>
         </ul> 
         <h1 id="epics">Epics <span class="badge-trigger premium"></span><a href="#epics" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h1> 
         <div class="introduced-in mb-3">
          Version history<button class="text-expander" type="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#release_version_notes_1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="release_version_notes_1" aria-label="Version history"></button>
          <div class="introduced-in-content collapse" id="release_version_notes_1"> 
           <ul> 
            <li>Introduced in <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/pricing/">GitLab Ultimate</a> 10.2. </li>
            <li>Single-level epics <a href="https://gitlab.com/gitlab-org/gitlab/-/issues/37081">were moved</a> to <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/pricing/">GitLab Premium</a> in 12.8. </li>
           </ul> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <p>When <a href="../../project/issues/index.html">issues</a> share a theme across projects and milestones, you can manage them by using epics. </p>
         <p>You can also create child epics, and assign start and end dates, which creates a visual roadmap for you to view progress. </p>
         <p>Use epics: </p>
         <ul> 
          <li>When your team is working on a large feature that involves multiple discussions in different issues in different projects in a <a href="../index.html">group</a>. </li>
          <li>To track when the work for the group of issues is targeted to begin and end. </li>
          <li>To discuss and collaborate on feature ideas and scope at a high level. </li>
         </ul> 
         <h2 id="relationships-between-epics-and-issues">Relationships between epics and issues<a href="#relationships-between-epics-and-issues" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>The possible relationships between epics and issues are: </p>
